    <script type="wix/htmlEmbeds" id="pageHtmlEmbeds.bodyStart end"></script>

<script id="wix-first-paint">
    if (window.ResizeObserver &&
        (!window.PerformanceObserver || !PerformanceObserver.supportedEntryTypes || PerformanceObserver.supportedEntryTypes.indexOf('paint') === -1)) {
        new ResizeObserver(function (entries, observer) {
            entries.some(function (entry) {
                var contentRect = entry.contentRect;
                if (contentRect.width > 0 && contentRect.height > 0) {
                    requestAnimationFrame(function (now) {
                        window.wixFirstPaint = now;
                        dispatchEvent(new CustomEvent('wixFirstPaint'));
                    });
                    observer.disconnect();
                    return true;
                }
            });
        }).observe(document.body);
    }
</script>

is a website dedicated to the topics of Cybersecurity and Mental Health.&nbsp; The resources presented herein are dedicated as How-Tos, blogs, technical information, and awareness regarding the darkness surrounding Mental Health whether it is a true mental illness or abuse disguised or mental illness.</span></p>

<p class="font_8 wixui-rich-text__text" style="font-size:16px;"><span class="wixui-rich-text__text"></span></p>

<p class="font_8 wixui-rich-text__text" style="font-size:16px;"><span class="color_11 wixui-rich-text__text">Regardless, Be Kind is always a good rule of thumb.&nbsp; You never know when you may be interacting with a traumatized human.</span></p>

<p class="wixui-rich-text__text">&nbsp;</p>

<p class="font_8 wixui-rich-text__text" style="font-size:16px;"><span class="wixui-rich-text__text"></span></p>

data-testid="richTextElement" ariaAttributes="[object Object]"><h3 class="font_4 wixui-rich-text__text" style="font-size:48px;"><span style="text-decoration:underline;" class="wixui-rich-text__text"><a href="https://www.cyberhands.tech/cybersecurity" target="_self" class="wixui-rich-text__text">Cybersecurity</a></span></h3></div><!--/$--><!--$--><div id="comp-luv9cty3" class="HcOXKn c9GqVL QxJLC3 lq2cno YQcXTT comp-luv9cty3 wixui-rich-text" data-testid="richTextElement" ariaAttributes="[object Object]"><p class="font_7 wixui-rich-text__text" style="font-size:20px;">Cybersecurity refers to the practice of protecting computer system, networks, data, and information systems from unauthorized access, cyber attacks, theft, damage, or any other form of cyber threats.&nbsp; It encompasses a wide range of technologies, processes, and practices designed to safeguard information and ensure the Confidentiality, Integrity, and Availability (CIA Triad) of digital assets.&nbsp; Simplified, Cybersecurity is protecting Data-at-Rest, Data-in-Transit, and Data-in-Use.</p></div><!--/$--></div></div></div><!--/$--><!--$--><div id="comp-luv9cty8" id="comp-luv9ctyq" class="HcOXKn c9GqVL QxJLC3 lq2cno YQcXTT comp-luv9ctyq wixui-rich-text" data-testid="richTextElement" ariaAttributes="[object Object]"><p class="font_7 wixui-rich-text__text"
